The GT has three basis functions:
1. `sqrt(A)` — a square root term
2. `A*exp(-0.0594*t)` — product of A and decaying exponential in t
3. `sin(0.5829*A)` — sine of A

**Key observations about GT structure:**
- Contains `sqrt(A)` — this is A^(1/2)
- Contains `A*exp(αt)` where α is negative
- Contains `sin(βA)` — sine function of A
- No polynomial terms in A (like A² or A), no constant term, no rational functions of A

Let me check candidates systematically:

**Candidate 1:** `A*c0/(A+c1) + c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*exp(c5*sin(c6*t+c7))`
